<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-faq" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#faq"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>FAQ</h1>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-how-do-the-presentation-slides-work" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-do-the-presentation-slides-work"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>How do the presentation slides work?</h3>
<p dir="auto">The presentation itself is a webpage hosted on GitHub. Basically, it
renders dynamically from a <a href="/Gibbons-Lab/isb_course_2021/blob/main/docs/16S/talk.md">markdown file that includes the course</a>.
Editing the markdown file is sufficient to change the content of the presentation.</p>
<p dir="auto">See the <a href="https://github.com/hakimel/reveal.js/#markdown">reveal docs</a> for more info.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-preview-locally" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#preview-locally"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Preview locally</h3>
<p dir="auto">Open a terminal in the <code>docs</code> folder in the repo and use:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="python -m http.server"><pre>python -m http.server</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This will preview the talks at <code>localhost:8000/16S</code> and <code>localhost:8000/models</code> in a browser. Editing the
markdown and reloading the page should be enough.</p>
<h3 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-pdf-output" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#pdf-output"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>PDF output</h3>
<p dir="auto">To generate a PDF of the course, open up the website in chromium or chrome and
append <code>?print-pdf</code> to the address. For instance, if you ran it locally as
described above, open <code>localhost:8000/16S?print-pdf</code> in the browser. Then, choose
'print to PDF' (choose margins: none).</p>
</article>
        </div>
    </div>

  </readme-toc>


</div>
